***wolk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wolk.html>wolk</a> (7432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wolke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wulko</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wulkô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolk.html>wolk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolken.html>wolken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolkje.html>wolkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cloud
<ol><li>visible mass of atmospheric water
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zon.html>zon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdween.html>verdween</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>achter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wolken.html>wolken</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Sun disappeared behind the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clouds.html>clouds</a></b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>visible mass of matter, in the medium air, resembling an atmospheric cloud</li>
<li>visible mass of matter in any medium, resembling an atmospheric cloud
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>Door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> gespartel <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertroebelen.html>vertroebelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> water <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wolken.html>wolken</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:konden.html>konden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>vissen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Because of the children's splashing the water got muddied with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clouds.html>clouds</a></b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> couldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> see any fish anymore.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol></li></ol>

***wolverine.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a> (17085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1619; alteration of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wolvering</i> (1574), diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wolver</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ravenous or savage animal; person who behaves like a <a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1593),<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> ultimately from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>wolf</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolverines.html>wolverines</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A solitary, fierce mammal of the Mustelidae family, <i><span class="Latn" lang="mul">Gulo gulo</span></i><sup><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gulo_gulo" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gulo gulo">ws</a></sup>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1920</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peter_B._Kyne" class="extiw" title="w:Peter B. Kyne"><a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> B. Kyne</a>,  chapter IV, in  <cite>The Understanding Heart</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“Wish I'd <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> more polite to that girl,” the <a href = vnd.unilang:sheriff.html>sheriff</a> remarked regretfully. “ I ain'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a bite to eat since four <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>'clock this morning, and I'm hungry as a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a></b>. … I know she'd have give <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> another <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> of that old <a href = vnd.unilang:moonshine.html>moonshine</a> she <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a>.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>carcajou, <a href = vnd.unilang:skunk.html>skunk</a> bear, glutton, quickhatch, beaver eater</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wonde.html>wonde</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wunde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wunda</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wundō</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wonderlijc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wunderlīk</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wonder</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wonderlijk.html>wonderlijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wonderlijker.html>wonderlijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">wonderlijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>miraculous, amazing</li>
<li>queer, odd</li>
<li>vagarious</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wonderlijk.html>wonderlijk</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:opmerkelijk.html>opmerkelijk</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ongewoon.html>ongewoon</a>

***woodcock.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a> (55387)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wodecocke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wode-koc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wodekok</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wudecocc</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wuducoc</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wood</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cock</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">woodcocks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several wading <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> in the genus <i>Scolopax</i>, of the family Scolopacidae, characterised by a long slender bill and cryptic brown and blackish plumage.</li>
<li>A simpleton.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1607–1611</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Beaumont" class="extiw" title="w:Francis Beaumont">Francis Beaumont</a> |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Fletcher_(playwright)" class="extiw" title="w:John Fletcher (playwright)">John <a href = vnd.unilang:fletcher.html>Fletcher</a></a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cupid%27s_Revenge" class="extiw" title="w:Cupid | s Revenge"><a href = vnd.unilang:cupid.html>Cupid</a>’s Revenge</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beaumont_and_Fletcher_folios" class="extiw" title="w:Beaumont and Fletcher folios">Comedies and <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Written by Francis Beavmont and Iohn Fletcher Gentlemen. Never Printed before, and Now Published by the Authours Originall Copies.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, London |  Printed for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Robinson" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Robinson">Humphrey Robinson</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Three Pidgeons">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, and for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphrey_Moseley" class="extiw" title="w:Humphrey Moseley">Humphrey Moseley</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="at the Princes Armes in St Pauls Church-yard.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, published 1679, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/3083972">3083972</a></small>, Act 4, scene 1:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>If I <a href = vnd.unilang:loved.html>loved</a> you not, I would laugh at you, and see you / Run your neck into the <a href = vnd.unilang:noose.html>noose</a>, and cry, "A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a></b>!"</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1838</b>, Nathan <a href = vnd.unilang:drake.html>Drake</a>, <i>Belletristical Works</i> (volume 1, page 215)
<dl><dd>"Now will that silly <b><a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a></b> make such a report of what I have <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> to his chosen friend," observed <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Robert to his companion when my Lord Cobham <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> out of hearing<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***woon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woon.html>woon</a> (1161)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wonen.html>wone</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woon.html>woon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">domicile</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">residence</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">home</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">abode</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">place of living</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">residence</span>, inhabiting <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">state of residing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woon.html>woon</a></strong>

***worden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> (123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:werthan.html>werthan</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*werþaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wértti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become; to get; to grow; to turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lerares.html>lerares</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She always <a href = vnd.unilang:wanted.html>wanted</a> to become a teacher.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:broer.html>broer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twintig.html>twintig</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">My brother <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> turning twenty today.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:benauwd.html>benauwd</a>. Open <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ramen.html>ramen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alsjeblieft.html>alsjeblieft</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It's getting very <a href = vnd.unilang:stuffy.html>stuffy</a> in here. Please open the <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>windows</a>!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form the imperfect tense of the passive voice, together with a past participle.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gered.html>gered</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They are being <a href = vnd.unilang:saved.html>saved</a>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschilderd.html>geschilderd</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The wall <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> being painted.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschilderd.html>geschilderd</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The wall will be painted. / The wall <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> going to be painted.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> tense passive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> formed using <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i>. The form <a href = vnd.unilang:matches.html>matches</a> English continuous constructions in meaning. Therefore, as in usage 2 above,</li></ul>
<ol><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gered.html>gered</a>.</i> translates to “They <b>are being</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:saved.html>saved</a>.”</li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gered.html>gered</a></i>. translates to “They <b><a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> being</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:saved.html>saved</a>.”</li>
<li>Consequently, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> </i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></b><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:gered.html>gered</a>.</i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> </i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a></b><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:gered.html>gered</a>.</i> would be <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> as “They <b>have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:saved.html>saved</a>.” and “They <b><a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:saved.html>saved</a>.” respectively.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a> (96750)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wormwode</i>, a folk etymology (as if <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">worm</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wood</i>) of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wermode</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wermōd</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wormōd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a>, absinthe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wermōdaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">wermode</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">wermede</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wermut</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:vermouth.html>vermouth</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">wormwoods</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An intensely bitter herb (<i>Artemisia absinthium</i> and similar plants in genus <i>Artemisia</i>) used in medicine, in the production of absinthe and <a href = vnd.unilang:vermouth.html>vermouth</a>, and as a <a href = vnd.unilang:tonic.html>tonic</a>.
<ul><li><b>ca. 1591–95</b>, William Shakespeare, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:romeo.html>Romeo</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:juliet.html>Juliet</a></i>, Act I, Scene iii <i>(the nurse's monologue)</i>.
<dl><dd>But as I <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>, / When it <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> taste the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></b> on the nipple / Of my dug and felt it bitter, pretty fool, / To see it tetchy and fall out with the dug!</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1611</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_James_Version" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:King James Version">King James Version</a>, Jeremiah 9:15:
<dl><dd>Therefore thus saith the Lord of hosts, the <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> of Israel; Behold, I will feed them, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> this people, with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></b>, and give them water of gall to <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li>ca. <b>1864</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Clare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Clare">John Clare</a>, "<a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> passed by green closes":
<dl><dd>Blue skippers in sunny <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ope.html>ope</a> and shut</dd>
<dd>Where <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></b> and grunsel flowers by the cart ruts <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1897</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edwin_Arlington_Robinson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edwin Arlington Robinson">Edwin Arlington Robinson</a>, <i>Children of the Night</i>, "<a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>Cliff</a> Klingenhagen":
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>Cliff</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> two glasses and filled one with wine</dd>
<dd>And one with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">grande <a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">absinthe</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">mugwort</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">artemisia</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Something that causes bitterness or affliction; a cause of mortification or vexation.
<ul><li><b>1789</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Moore_(Scottish_physician)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Moore (Scottish physician)">John Moore</a>, <i>Zeluco</i>, Valancourt 2008, p. 57:
<dl><dd>The irony of this reply <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></b> to Zeluco; he fell into a gloomy fit of musing, and made no farther inquiry <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 3; -moz-column-count: 3; -ms-column-count: 3; -o-column-count: 3; -webkit-column-count: 3;">
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/common_wormwood" class="extiw" title="w:common wormwood">common <a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></a></li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/tree_wormwood" class="extiw" title="w:tree wormwood">tree <a href = vnd.unilang:wormwood.html>wormwood</a></a></li>

</div>
</body>

***worstel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:worstel.html>worstel</a> (22954)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***wortel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wortel.html>wortel</a> (6828)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wortelen.html>wortele</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wurtala</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wurt-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">root</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*waluz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, formed from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> roots <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wréh₂ds</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*WelH-</i>. The mathematical sense <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simon_Stevin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Simon Stevin"><a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> Stevin</a>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wurzel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Wuddel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:wortel.html>Wortel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">woartel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wyrtwalu</i>; cf. also English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wort</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wortel.html>wortel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wortels.html>wortels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wortelen.html>wortelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:worteltje.html>worteltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>carrot</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wortel.html>wortel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wortels.html>wortels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:worteltje.html>worteltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>root (especially of a plant)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> square root, root</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> zero of a function, root</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***woud.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:woud.html>woud</a> (7679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wout.html>wout</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:walt.html>walt</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*walþuz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woud.html>woud</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wouden.html>wouden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woud.html>woudje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>forest, woods, <a href = vnd.unilang:jungle.html>jungle</a>
<ul><li><b>1778</b>, Thomas Harmer, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:waarnemingen.html>Waarnemingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oosten.html>Oosten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> reisbeschrijvingen, <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opheldering.html>opheldering</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> </i><a href = vnd.unilang:heilige.html>Heilige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schrift.html>Schrift</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> from English, with comments by "<a href = vnd.unilang:johan.html>Johan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ernst.html>Ernst</a> Faber" (= Johann <a href = vnd.unilang:ernst.html>Ernst</a> Faber), <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> from German, publ. by G. <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Paddenburg, second book, page 237.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>Toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vond.html>vond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> veele <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wouden.html>wouden</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:waarvan.html>waarvan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dezen.html>dezen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> verſcheidenen <a href = vnd.unilang:overig.html>overig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebleven.html>gebleven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> (12). <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>Uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zulke.html>zulke</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wouden.html>wouden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:haalden.html>haalden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> dorpſchappen <a href = vnd.unilang:hunnen.html>hunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wanneer.html>wanneer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> Aleppo <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfs.html>zelfs</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> houwboſſchen <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Back then there <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> still many <b>forests</b>, of which several remain up to this day (12). From <b>forests</b> like these the villages <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> firewood when they, as <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the case around Aleppo itself, didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> have any coppices for firewood.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***wouw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wouw.html>wouw</a> (50215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wouwe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wīwe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wīe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīwô</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weihe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Wieh</i>, both “harrier”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wouw.html>wouw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wouw.html>wouwen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wouw.html>wouwtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A kite, certain bird of the family Accipitridae; especially of the genera <i>Milvus</i>, <i>Harpagus</i> and <i>Haliastur</i>.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wraak.html>wraak</a> (1521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wrāke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wraeck</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wrāka</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wrāca</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wrēkō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">persecution, revenge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wreg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drive, press, urge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wrack</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wreak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vengeance, revenge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:rache.html>Rache</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">revenge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">wreak</span>.

***wraith.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wraith.html>wraith</a> (6870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested 1513, in a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Scots" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Scots">Middle Scots</a></span> translation of the Aeneid.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p><p>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> no certain etymology. J. <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. Tolkien favored a link with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">writhe</i>. Also compared are <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">warth</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">vǫrðr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">watcher, guardian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">vörður</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">guard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wray.html>wray</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bewray</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wreien</i>. Perhaps from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wrath</i> as a <a href = vnd.unilang:wraith.html>wraith</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a vengeful spirit.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wraith.html>wraith</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">wraiths</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A ghost or specter, especially a person's likeness seen just after their death.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">ghost</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1912</b> February–July,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edgar_Rice_Burroughs" class="extiw" title="w:Edgar Rice Burroughs"><a href = vnd.unilang:edgar.html>Edgar</a> Rice Burroughs</a>,  “Under the <a href = vnd.unilang:moons.html>Moons</a> of Mars”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Argosy_(magazine)The_All-Story" class="extiw" title="w:Argosy (magazine)">The All-Story</a></cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frank_Munsey" class="extiw" title="w:Frank Munsey"><a href = vnd.unilang:frank.html>Frank</a> A. Munsey Co.</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/17392886">17392886</a></small> |  republished as  “Sola <a href = vnd.unilang:tells.html>Tells</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>Me</a> Her Story”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Princess_of_Mars" class="extiw" title="w:A Princess of Mars">A Princess of <a href = vnd.unilang:mars.html>Mars</a></a></cite>, Chicago, Ill. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A._C._McClurg" class="extiw" title="w:A. C. McClurg">A[lexander] C[aldwell] McClurg amp; Co.</a>, 1917, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/419578288">419578288</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://babel.hathitrust.org/cgi/pt?id=osu.32435018239657amp;view=1upamp;seq=185">pages 159–160</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> might indeed have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> the <b>wraiths</b> of the departed dead upon the dead sea of that dying planet for all the sound or sign <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> made in passing.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2001</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joyce_Carol_Oates" class="extiw" title="w:Joyce Carol Oates">Joyce <a href = vnd.unilang:carol.html>Carol</a> Oates</a>,  <cite>Middle Age: A Romance</cite>, paperback edition, Fourth Estate, page 80:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Like <b>wraiths</b> with the impediments of <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a> they stumbled in the direction of Salthill <a href = vnd.unilang:faces.html>faces</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">wraithish</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">wraithful</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">wraithlike</span></li></ul>
</body> 
***wrak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wrak.html>wrak</a> (4984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wrac</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">defective; wreck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wrekaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to push, drive out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably in the sense of <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> cast ashore.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wrak.html>wrak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wrakken.html>wrakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wrak.html>wrakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A wreck <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a> of a vehicle, vessel, aircraft or other piece of machinery</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ten <a href = vnd.unilang:strengste.html>strengste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verboden.html>verboden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wrak.html>wrak</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naast.html>naast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koraalrif.html>koraalrif</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betreden.html>betreden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> strictly prohibited to enter the <b>wreck</b> next to the coral reef.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A wreck <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">severely damaged creature</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:henk.html>Henk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wrak.html>wrak</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:anna.html>Anna</a>'s <a href = vnd.unilang:overlijden.html>overlijden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:henk.html>Henk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> an <b>emotional wreck</b> after <a href = vnd.unilang:anna.html>Anna</a>'s death.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wrak.html>wrak</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-5"> | 5 | </a></sup>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wrake.html>wrake</a> (32875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:wrake.html>wrake</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vengeance, persecution, injury</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ƿracu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">revenge, persecution, misery, etc.</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wrakō</i>, likely related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wrēkō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">persecution, revenge, vengeance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍅𐍂𐌰𐌺𐌰</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">wraka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">persecution</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:wrake.html>wrake</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wrake.html>wrake</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wrake.html>wrake</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">wrakes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Suffering which <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> as a result of vengeance or retribution.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wrack</i>.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wrat.html>wrat</a> (25502)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wratte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wratt</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wratta</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*warta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wartǭ</i>. The phonetic development <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> irregular, but compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">wratte</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wrette</i>. Some modern Dutch dialects have the expected form <i>wa(a)rt</i>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Warze</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wart</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wrat.html>wrat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zwijn.html>zwijn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***wray.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wray.html>wray</a> (25075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wrayen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wraien</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wreien</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to show, make known, accuse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wrēġan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to urge, incite, stir up, accuse, impeach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wrōgijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tell; tell on; announce; accuse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*were-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wrē-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tell; speak; shout</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wroegen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blame</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">rügen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to reprove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">röja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bewray; reveal; expose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wray.html>wray</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">wrays</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">wraying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">wrayed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To denounce (a person).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To reveal (a secret).
<ul><li><b>1387-1400</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Geoffrey_Chaucer" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Geoffrey Chaucer">Geoffrey Chaucer</a>, "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Franklin%27s_Tale" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Franklin | s Tale">The Franklin's Tale</a>", <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canterbury_Tales" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Canterbury Tales">Canterbury Tales</a></i>
<dl><dd>no thyng <a href = vnd.unilang:dor.html>dorste</a> he seye, / Save in his songes somwhat wolde he <b>wreye</b> / His wo</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To betray.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Geoffrey Chaucer and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>, <i>The Miller's Tale</i>.
<dl><dd>Thou shalt upon thy trouthe swere <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heere.html>heere</a></dd>
<dd>That to no <a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a> thou shalt this conseil <b>wreye</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wreef.html>wreef</a> (27847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wrijch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">instep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from Proto-Germanic *wrīha(n)<a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a>. Most likely influenced by the Dutch verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wrijven.html>wrijven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rub</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with Old High German <i class="None mention" lang="gho">rīho</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knee; back of knee</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from which dialectal German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Reihen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">instep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
